- Financing should use **current home equity**.

2) **Soft Constraints**
- Aim for family-oriented neighborhoods with access to amenities (parks, schools, etc.).
- Preference for homes in good condition to minimize renovation needs.
- Ideally detached or semi-detached homes with a yard.
- Reasonable proximity to work or transit (if applicable).

3) **Task Decomposition**
   a) **Property Search**
      - Ask the external agent (real estate agent) to find 4+ bedroom family homes in Oakville within CAD $850–950K, located in good school districts.
      - Get details such as address, property type, size, year built, and price.
   b) **Financing Solutions**
      - Explore mortgage options, specifically using home equity.
      - Request terms (interest rate, amortization period, down payment requirements).
   c) **Legal Services Coordination**
      - Find legal service providers specializing in property purchases in Ontario.
      - Obtain estimated costs for closing, title transfer, and property survey.
   d) **Moving Services**
      - Identify local moving companies and get cost estimates for relocation.
   e) **Setup & Utilities**
      - Arrange or estimate initial setup for utilities (electricity, internet, water, gas).
   f) **Budget Summary**
      - Compile total costs: property price + closing/legal fees + moving costs + setup fees.

4) **Data Planning (Information Needed from Environment)**
   - User’s full name and David’s relationship (spouse/partner confirmation).
   - Current home equity amount or approximate value to calculate financing.
   - Current address (to help plan move and financing).
   - Contact email or phone for follow-ups with external professionals.

5) **Anticipated Changes**
   - Budget flexibility if suitable properties are slightly above CAD $950K but offer significant value.
   - Adjust financing terms depending on home equity results.
   - Modify service selections based on availability and cost from external providers.

</initial_plan>
